<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проваливавшийся.html>прова́ливавшийся</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proválivavšijsja</span>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провалить.html>провали́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">provalítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проваливать.html>прова́ливать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proválivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провалить.html>провали́ть</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проваливаться.html>прова́ливаться</a> (7935)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проваливать.html>прова́ливать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">proválivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проваливаться.html>прова́ливаться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proválivatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провалиться.html>провали́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fall through, to come down</li>
<li>to fail, to flunk (on an exam)</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проваливать.html>прова́ливать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">proválivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***провалить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:провалить.html>провали́ть</a> (17118)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:валить.html>вали́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">valítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провалить.html>провали́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">provalítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проваливать.html>прова́ливать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to botch up, to ruin, to mess up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:провалить.html>провали́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ло</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>provalítʹ</b> délo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to ruin things; make a mess of things; mess things up; gum up the works</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:провалить.html>провали́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:роль.html>роль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>provalítʹ</b> rolʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to ruin ones part</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:провалить.html>провали́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:экзамен.html>экза́мен</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>provalítʹ</b> ekzámen</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fail/flunk an exam</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fail
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:провалить.html>провали́ть</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:письменный.html>пи́сьменном</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:экзамен.html>экза́мене</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>provalítʹ</b> kovó-libo na písʹmennom ekzámene</i> ― <span class="e-translation">fail smb in the written paper</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оппозиция.html>оппози́ция</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:провалить.html>провали́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:план.html>план</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:правительство.html>прави́тельства</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">oppozícija <b>provalíla</b> plan pravítelʹstva</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the opposition torpedoed the government's plan</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:провалить.html>провали́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:законопроект.html>законопрое́кт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>provalítʹ</b> zakonoproékt</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to kill the bill</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:провалить.html>провали́ть</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голосование.html>голосова́нии</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>provalítʹ</b> kovó-libo pri golosovánii</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to vote smb down</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провалить.html>провали́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">provalítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провалиться.html>провали́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">provalítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проваливаться.html>прова́ливаться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fall through, to come down
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потолок.html>потоло́к</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:провалиться.html>провали́лся</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">potolók <b>provalílsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the ceiling has come down</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сквозь.html>сквозь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:земля.html>зе́млю</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:провалиться.html>провали́лся</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kak skvozʹ zémlju <b>provalílsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">vanished into thin air</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:провалиться.html>провали́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́том</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сте</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:если.html>е́сли</a> ...</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>provalítʹsja</b> mne na étom méste, jésli ...</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I'll be damned if ...</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to fail, to flunk (on an exam)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:провалиться.html>провали́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:треск.html>тре́ском</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>provalítʹsja</b> s tréskom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to turn out a complete fiasco</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провалить.html>провали́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">provalítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведать.html>ве́дать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">védatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проведать.html>прове́дать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">provédatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">прове́дывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to come to see, to call <i>(on)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to find out, to learn <i>(of, about)</i></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проведение.html>проведе́ние</a> (3447)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проводить.html>проводи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">provodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проведение.html>проведе́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">provedénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проведение.html>проведе́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проведение.html>проведе́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проведение.html>проведе́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>construction, building, laying <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of roads, cables, pipes, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>organization, holding <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a meeting, event, activity</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>carrying out, realization, implementation</li>
<li>adoption <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a resolution, law</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:провернуть.html>проверну́ть</a> (19757)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вернуть.html>верну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vernútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провернуть.html>проверну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">provernútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">провёртывать</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проворачивать.html>провора́чивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to drill a hole in, to perforate</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to twist (something) through (something) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">esp. meat through a meat grinder</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to crank</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to turn with difficulty</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to quickly do or arrange</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">провороти́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">provorotítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">low colloquial register</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">except for "to quickly do"</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">проверте́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">provertétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">colloquial register</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ul>
